    10	/// A parsed sentinel word indicating the type of directive to be parsed next.
    11	#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Hash, Eq, PartialEq)]
    12	#[cfg_attr(test, derive(strum::EnumIter))]
    13	pub(crate) enum DirectiveKind {
    14	    /// A [`crate::diagnostic_filter`].
    15	    Diagnostic,
    16	    /// An [`enable_extension`].
    17	    Enable,
    18	    /// A [`language_extension`].
    19	    Requires,
    20	}
    21	
    22	impl DirectiveKind {
    23	    const DIAGNOSTIC: &'static str = "diagnostic";
    24	    const ENABLE: &'static str = "enable";
    25	    const REQUIRES: &'static str = "requires";
    26	
    27	    /// Convert from a sentinel word in WGSL into its associated [`DirectiveKind`], if possible.
    28	    pub fn from_ident(s: &str) -> Option<Self> {
    29	        Some(match s {
    30	            Self::DIAGNOSTIC => Self::Diagnostic,
    31	            Self::ENABLE => Self::Enable,
    32	            Self::REQUIRES => Self::Requires,
    33	            _ => return None,
    34	        })
    35	    }
    36	}
    37	
    38	impl crate::diagnostic_filter::Severity {
    39	    #[cfg(feature = "wgsl-in")]
    40	    pub(crate) fn report_wgsl_parse_diag<'a>(
    41	        self,
    42	        err: Box<crate::front::wgsl::error::Error<'a>>,
    43	        source: &str,
    44	    ) -> crate::front::wgsl::Result<'a, ()> {
    45	        self.report_diag(err, |e, level| {
    46	            let e = e.as_parse_error(source);
    47	            log::log!(level, "{}", e.emit_to_string(source));
    48	        })
    49	    }
    50	}

    61	    #[test]
    62	    fn directive_after_global_decl() {
    63	        for unsupported_shader in DirectiveKind::iter() {
    64	            let directive;
    65	            let expected_msg;
    66	            match unsupported_shader {
    67	                DirectiveKind::Diagnostic => {
    68	                    directive = "diagnostic(off,derivative_uniformity)";
    69	                    expected_msg = "\
    70	error: expected global declaration, but found a global directive
    71	  ┌─ wgsl:2:1
    72	  │
    73	2 │ diagnostic(off,derivative_uniformity);
    74	  │ ^^^^^^^^^^ written after first global declaration
    75	  │
    76	  = note: global directives are only allowed before global declarations; maybe hoist this closer to the top of the shader module?
    77	
    78	";
    79	                }
    80	                DirectiveKind::Enable => {
    81	                    directive = "enable f16";
    82	                    expected_msg = "\
    83	error: expected global declaration, but found a global directive
    84	  ┌─ wgsl:2:1
    85	  │
    86	2 │ enable f16;
    87	  │ ^^^^^^ written after first global declaration
    88	  │
    89	  = note: global directives are only allowed before global declarations; maybe hoist this closer to the top of the shader module?
    90	
    91	";
    92	                }
    93	                DirectiveKind::Requires => {
    94	                    directive = "requires readonly_and_readwrite_storage_textures";
    95	                    expected_msg = "\
    96	error: expected global declaration, but found a global directive
    97	  ┌─ wgsl:2:1
    98	  │
    99	2 │ requires readonly_and_readwrite_storage_textures;
   100	  │ ^^^^^^^^ written after first global declaration
   101	  │
   102	  = note: global directives are only allowed before global declarations; maybe hoist this closer to the top of the shader module?
   103	
   104	";
   105	                }
   106	            }
   107	
   108	            let shader = format!(
   109	                "\
   110	@group(0) @binding(0) var<storage> thing: i32;
   111	{directive};
   112	"
   113	            );
   114	            assert_parse_err(&shader, expected_msg);
   115	        }
   116	    }

     1	//! `enable …;` extensions in WGSL.
     2	//!
     3	//! The focal point of this module is the [`EnableExtension`] API.
     4	
     5	use crate::front::wgsl::{Error, Result};
     6	use crate::Span;
     7	
     8	use alloc::boxed::Box;
     9	
    10	/// Tracks the status of every enable-extension known to Naga.
    11	#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, PartialEq)]
    12	pub(crate) struct EnableExtensions {
    13	    wgpu_mesh_shader: bool,
    14	    wgpu_ray_query: bool,
    15	    wgpu_ray_query_vertex_return: bool,
    16	    wgpu_ray_tracing_pipelines: bool,
    17	    dual_source_blending: bool,
    18	    /// Whether `enable f16;` was written earlier in the shader module.
    19	    f16: bool,
    20	    clip_distances: bool,
    21	    wgpu_cooperative_matrix: bool,
    22	    draw_index: bool,
    23	    primitive_index: bool,
    24	    per_vertex: bool,
    25	}
    26	
    27	impl EnableExtensions {
    28	    pub(crate) const fn empty() -> Self {
    29	        Self {
    30	            wgpu_mesh_shader: false,
    31	            wgpu_ray_query: false,
    32	            wgpu_ray_query_vertex_return: false,
    33	            wgpu_ray_tracing_pipelines: false,
    34	            f16: false,
    35	            dual_source_blending: false,
    36	            clip_distances: false,
    37	            wgpu_cooperative_matrix: false,
    38	            draw_index: false,
    39	            primitive_index: false,
    40	            per_vertex: false,
    41	        }
    42	    }
    43	
    44	    /// Add an enable-extension to the set requested by a module.
    45	    pub(crate) const fn add(&mut self, ext: ImplementedEnableExtension) {
    46	        let field = match ext {
    47	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuMeshShader => &mut self.wgpu_mesh_shader,
    48	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQuery => &mut self.wgpu_ray_query,
    49	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn => {
    50	                &mut self.wgpu_ray_query_vertex_return
    51	            }
    52	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline => {
    53	                &mut self.wgpu_ray_tracing_pipelines
    54	            }
    55	            ImplementedEnableExtension::DualSourceBlending => &mut self.dual_source_blending,
    56	            ImplementedEnableExtension::F16 => &mut self.f16,
    57	            ImplementedEnableExtension::ClipDistances => &mut self.clip_distances,
    58	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuCooperativeMatrix => &mut self.wgpu_cooperative_matrix,
    59	            ImplementedEnableExtension::DrawIndex => &mut self.draw_index,
    60	            ImplementedEnableExtension::PrimitiveIndex => &mut self.primitive_index,
    61	            ImplementedEnableExtension::PerVertex => &mut self.per_vertex,
    62	        };
    63	        *field = true;
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    /// Query whether an enable-extension tracked here has been requested.
    67	    pub(crate) const fn contains(&self, ext: ImplementedEnableExtension) -> bool {
    68	        match ext {
    69	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuMeshShader => self.wgpu_mesh_shader,
    70	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQuery => self.wgpu_ray_query,
    71	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn => {
    72	                self.wgpu_ray_query_vertex_return
    73	            }
    74	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline => self.wgpu_ray_tracing_pipelines,
    75	            ImplementedEnableExtension::DualSourceBlending => self.dual_source_blending,
    76	            ImplementedEnableExtension::F16 => self.f16,
    77	            ImplementedEnableExtension::ClipDistances => self.clip_distances,
    78	            ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuCooperativeMatrix => self.wgpu_cooperative_matrix,
    79	            ImplementedEnableExtension::DrawIndex => self.draw_index,
    80	            ImplementedEnableExtension::PrimitiveIndex => self.primitive_index,
    81	            ImplementedEnableExtension::PerVertex => self.per_vertex,
    82	        }
    83	    }
    84	
    85	    pub(crate) fn require(
    86	        &self,
    87	        ext: ImplementedEnableExtension,
    88	        span: Span,
    89	    ) -> Result<'static, ()> {
    90	        if !self.contains(ext) {
    91	            Err(Box::new(Error::EnableExtensionNotEnabled {
    92	                span,
    93	                kind: ext.into(),
    94	            }))
    95	        } else {
    96	            Ok(())
    97	        }
    98	    }
    99	}
   100	
   101	impl Default for EnableExtensions {
   102	    fn default() -> Self {
   103	        Self::empty()
   104	    }
   105	}
   106	
   107	/// An enable-extension not guaranteed to be present in all environments.
   108	///
   109	/// WGSL spec.: <https://www.w3.org/TR/WGSL/#enable-extensions-sec>
   110	#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Hash, Eq, PartialEq)]
   111	pub enum EnableExtension {
   112	    Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension),
   113	    Unimplemented(UnimplementedEnableExtension),
   114	}
   115	
   116	impl From<ImplementedEnableExtension> for EnableExtension {
   117	    fn from(value: ImplementedEnableExtension) -> Self {
   118	        Self::Implemented(value)
   119	    }
   120	}
   121	
   122	impl EnableExtension {
   123	    const F16: &'static str = "f16";
   124	    const CLIP_DISTANCES: &'static str = "clip_distances";
   125	    const DUAL_SOURCE_BLENDING: &'static str = "dual_source_blending";
   126	    const MESH_SHADER: &'static str = "wgpu_mesh_shader";
   127	    const RAY_QUERY: &'static str = "wgpu_ray_query";
   128	    const RAY_QUERY_VERTEX_RETURN: &'static str = "wgpu_ray_query_vertex_return";
   129	    const RAY_TRACING_PIPELINE: &'static str = "wgpu_ray_tracing_pipeline";
   130	    const COOPERATIVE_MATRIX: &'static str = "wgpu_cooperative_matrix";
   131	    const SUBGROUPS: &'static str = "subgroups";
   132	    const PRIMITIVE_INDEX: &'static str = "primitive_index";
   133	    const DRAW_INDEX: &'static str = "draw_index";
   134	    const PER_VERTEX: &'static str = "wgpu_per_vertex";
   135	
   136	    /// Convert from a sentinel word in WGSL into its associated [`EnableExtension`], if possible.
   137	    pub(crate) fn from_ident(word: &str, span: Span) -> Result<'_, Self> {
   138	        Ok(match word {
   139	            Self::F16 => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::F16),
   140	            Self::CLIP_DISTANCES => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::ClipDistances),
   141	            Self::DUAL_SOURCE_BLENDING => {
   142	                Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::DualSourceBlending)
   143	            }
   144	            Self::MESH_SHADER => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuMeshShader),
   145	            Self::RAY_QUERY => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQuery),
   146	            Self::RAY_QUERY_VERTEX_RETURN => {
   147	                Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn)
   148	            }
   149	            Self::RAY_TRACING_PIPELINE => {
   150	                Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline)
   151	            }
   152	            Self::COOPERATIVE_MATRIX => {
   153	                Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuCooperativeMatrix)
   154	            }
   155	            Self::SUBGROUPS => Self::Unimplemented(UnimplementedEnableExtension::Subgroups),
   156	            Self::DRAW_INDEX => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::DrawIndex),
   157	            Self::PRIMITIVE_INDEX => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::PrimitiveIndex),
   158	            Self::PER_VERTEX => Self::Implemented(ImplementedEnableExtension::PerVertex),
   159	            _ => return Err(Box::new(Error::UnknownEnableExtension(span, word))),
   160	        })
   161	    }
   162	
   163	    /// Maps this [`EnableExtension`] into the sentinel word associated with it in WGSL.
   164	    pub const fn to_ident(self) -> &'static str {
   165	        match self {
   166	            Self::Implemented(kind) => match kind {
   167	                ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuMeshShader => Self::MESH_SHADER,
   168	                ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQuery => Self::RAY_QUERY,
   169	                ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn => {
   170	                    Self::RAY_QUERY_VERTEX_RETURN
   171	                }
   172	                ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuCooperativeMatrix => Self::COOPERATIVE_MATRIX,
   173	                ImplementedEnableExtension::DualSourceBlending => Self::DUAL_SOURCE_BLENDING,
   174	                ImplementedEnableExtension::F16 => Self::F16,
   175	                ImplementedEnableExtension::ClipDistances => Self::CLIP_DISTANCES,
   176	                ImplementedEnableExtension::DrawIndex => Self::DRAW_INDEX,
   177	                ImplementedEnableExtension::PrimitiveIndex => Self::PRIMITIVE_INDEX,
   178	                ImplementedEnableExtension::WgpuRayTracingPipeline => Self::RAY_TRACING_PIPELINE,
   179	                ImplementedEnableExtension::PerVertex => Self::PER_VERTEX,
   180	            },
   181	            Self::Unimplemented(kind) => match kind {
   182	                UnimplementedEnableExtension::Subgroups => Self::SUBGROUPS,
   183	            },
   184	        }
   185	    }
   186	}
   187	
   188	/// A variant of [`EnableExtension::Implemented`].
   189	#[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Hash, Eq, PartialEq)]
   190	#[cfg_attr(test, derive(strum::VariantArray))]
   191	pub enum ImplementedEnableExtension {
   192	    /// Enables `f16`/`half` primitive support in all shader languages.
   193	    ///
   194	    /// In the WGSL standard, this corresponds to [`enable f16;`].
   195	    ///
   196	    /// [`enable f16;`]: https://www.w3.org/TR/WGSL/#extension-f16
   197	    F16,
   198	    /// Enables the `blend_src` attribute in WGSL.
   199	    ///
   200	    /// In the WGSL standard, this corresponds to [`enable dual_source_blending;`].
   201	    ///
   202	    /// [`enable dual_source_blending;`]: https://www.w3.org/TR/WGSL/#extension-dual_source_blending
   203	    DualSourceBlending,
   204	    /// Enables the `clip_distances` variable in WGSL.
   205	    ///
   206	    /// In the WGSL standard, this corresponds to [`enable clip_distances;`].
   207	    ///
   208	    /// [`enable clip_distances;`]: https://www.w3.org/TR/WGSL/#extension-clip_distances
   209	    ClipDistances,
   210	    /// Enables the `wgpu_mesh_shader` extension, native only
   211	    WgpuMeshShader,
   212	    /// Enables the `wgpu_ray_query` extension, native only.
   213	    WgpuRayQuery,
   214	    /// Enables the `wgpu_ray_query_vertex_return` extension, native only.
   215	    WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn,
   216	    /// Enables the `wgpu_ray_tracing_pipeline` extension, native only.
   217	    WgpuRayTracingPipeline,
   218	    /// Enables the `wgpu_cooperative_matrix` extension, native only.
   219	    WgpuCooperativeMatrix,
   220	    /// Enables the `draw_index` builtin. Not currently part of the WGSL spec but probably will be at some point.
   221	    DrawIndex,
   222	    /// Enables the `@builtin(primitive_index)` attribute in WGSL.
   223	    ///
   224	    /// In the WGSL standard, this corresponds to [`enable primitive-index;`].
   225	    ///
   226	    /// [`enable primitive-index;`]: https://www.w3.org/TR/WGSL/#extension-primitive_index
   227	    PrimitiveIndex,
   228	    /// Enables the `wgpu_per_vertex` extension, allows using `@interpolate(per_vertex)` attribute in WGSL, native only.
   229	    PerVertex,
   230	}
   231	
   232	impl ImplementedEnableExtension {
   233	    /// A slice of all variants of [`ImplementedEnableExtension`].
   234	    pub const VARIANTS: &'static [Self] = &[
   235	        Self::F16,
   236	        Self::DualSourceBlending,
   237	        Self::ClipDistances,
   238	        Self::WgpuMeshShader,
   239	        Self::WgpuRayQuery,
   240	        Self::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn,
   241	        Self::WgpuRayTracingPipeline,
   242	        Self::WgpuCooperativeMatrix,
   243	        Self::DrawIndex,
   244	        Self::PrimitiveIndex,
   245	        Self::PerVertex,
   246	    ];
   247	
   248	    /// Returns slice of all variants of [`ImplementedEnableExtension`].
   249	    pub const fn all() -> &'static [Self] {
   250	        Self::VARIANTS
   251	    }
   252	
   253	    /// Returns the capability required for this enable extension.
   254	    pub const fn capability(self) -> crate::valid::Capabilities {
   255	        use crate::valid::Capabilities as C;
   256	        match self {
   257	            Self::F16 => C::SHADER_FLOAT16,

   259	            Self::ClipDistances => C::CLIP_DISTANCES,

   266	            Self::PrimitiveIndex => C::PRIMITIVE_INDEX,
   267	            Self::PerVertex => C::PER_VERTEX,
   268	        }
   269	    }

   363	        "unpack4xU8" => Mf::Unpack4xU8,
   364	        _ => return None,
   365	    })
   366	}
   367	
   368	pub fn map_conservative_depth(word: &str, span: Span) -> Result<'_, crate::ConservativeDepth> {
   369	    use crate::ConservativeDepth as Cd;
   370	    match word {
   371	        "greater_equal" => Ok(Cd::GreaterEqual),
   372	        "less_equal" => Ok(Cd::LessEqual),
   373	        "unchanged" => Ok(Cd::Unchanged),
   374	        _ => Err(Box::new(Error::UnknownConservativeDepth(span))),
   375	    }
   376	}
   377	
   378	pub fn map_subgroup_operation(
   379	    word: &str,
   380	) -> Option<(crate::SubgroupOperation, crate::CollectiveOperation)> {
   381	    use crate::CollectiveOperation as co;
   382	    use crate::SubgroupOperation as sg;
   383	    Some(match word {
   384	        "subgroupAll" => (sg::All, co::Reduce),
   385	        "subgroupAny" => (sg::Any, co::Reduce),
   386	        "subgroupAdd" => (sg::Add, co::Reduce),
   387	        "subgroupMul" => (sg::Mul, co::Reduce),
   388	        "subgroupMin" => (sg::Min, co::Reduce),
   389	        "subgroupMax" => (sg::Max, co::Reduce),
   390	        "subgroupAnd" => (sg::And, co::Reduce),
   391	        "subgroupOr" => (sg::Or, co::Reduce),
   392	        "subgroupXor" => (sg::Xor, co::Reduce),
   393	        "subgroupExclusiveAdd" => (sg::Add, co::ExclusiveScan),
   394	        "subgroupExclusiveMul" => (sg::Mul, co::ExclusiveScan),
   395	        "subgroupInclusiveAdd" => (sg::Add, co::InclusiveScan),
   396	        "subgroupInclusiveMul" => (sg::Mul, co::InclusiveScan),
   397	        _ => return None,
   398	    })
   399	}

   236	            Self::RAY_QUERY => Some(Ext::WgpuRayQuery),
   237	            Self::RAY_HIT_VERTEX_POSITION => Some(Ext::WgpuRayQueryVertexReturn),
   238	            Self::COOPERATIVE_MATRIX => Some(Ext::WgpuCooperativeMatrix),
   239	            Self::RAY_TRACING_PIPELINE => Some(Ext::WgpuRayTracingPipeline),
   240	            Self::PER_VERTEX => Some(Ext::PerVertex),
   241	            _ => None,
   242	        }
   243	    }
   244	}
   245	
   246	impl Default for Capabilities {
   247	    fn default() -> Self {
   248	        Self::MULTISAMPLED_SHADING | Self::CUBE_ARRAY_TEXTURES
   249	    }
   250	}
   251	
   252	bitflags::bitflags! {
   253	    /// Supported subgroup operations
   254	    #[cfg_attr(feature = "serialize", derive(serde::Serialize))]
   255	    #[cfg_attr(feature = "deserialize", derive(serde::Deserialize))]
   256	    #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Default, Eq, PartialEq)]
   257	    pub struct SubgroupOperationSet: u8 {
   258	        /// Barriers
   259	        // Possibly elections, when that is supported.
   260	        // https://github.com/gfx-rs/wgpu/issues/6042#issuecomment-3272603431
   261	        // Contrary to what the name "basic" suggests, HLSL/DX12 support the
   262	        // other subgroup operations, but do not support subgroup barriers.
   263	        const BASIC = 1 << 0;
   264	        /// Any, All
   265	        const VOTE = 1 << 1;
   266	        /// reductions, scans
   267	        const ARITHMETIC = 1 << 2;
   268	        /// ballot, broadcast
   269	        const BALLOT = 1 << 3;
   270	        /// shuffle, shuffle xor
   271	        const SHUFFLE = 1 << 4;
   272	        /// shuffle up, down
   273	        const SHUFFLE_RELATIVE = 1 << 5;
   274	        // We don't support these operations yet
   275	        // /// Clustered
   276	        // const CLUSTERED = 1 << 6;
   277	        /// Quad supported
   278	        const QUAD_FRAGMENT_COMPUTE = 1 << 7;
   279	        // /// Quad supported in all stages
   280	        // const QUAD_ALL_STAGES = 1 << 8;
   281	    }
   282	}
   283	
   284	impl super::SubgroupOperation {
   285	    const fn required_operations(&self) -> SubgroupOperationSet {
   286	        use SubgroupOperationSet as S;
   287	        match *self {
   288	            Self::All | Self::Any => S::VOTE,
   289	            Self::Add | Self::Mul | Self::Min | Self::Max | Self::And | Self::Or | Self::Xor => {
   290	                S::ARITHMETIC
   291	            }
   292	        }
   293	    }
   294	}
   295	
   296	impl super::GatherMode {
   297	    const fn required_operations(&self) -> SubgroupOperationSet {
   298	        use SubgroupOperationSet as S;
   299	        match *self {
   300	            Self::BroadcastFirst | Self::Broadcast(_) => S::BALLOT,
   301	            Self::Shuffle(_) | Self::ShuffleXor(_) => S::SHUFFLE,
   302	            Self::ShuffleUp(_) | Self::ShuffleDown(_) => S::SHUFFLE_RELATIVE,
   303	            Self::QuadBroadcast(_) | Self::QuadSwap(_) => S::QUAD_FRAGMENT_COMPUTE,
   304	        }
   305	    }
   306	}
   307	
   308	bitflags::bitflags! {
   309	    /// Validation flags.
   310	    #[cfg_attr(feature = "serialize", derive(serde::Serialize))]
   311	    #[cfg_attr(feature = "deserialize", derive(serde::Deserialize))]
   312	    #[derive(Clone, Copy, Debug, Eq, PartialEq)]
   313	    pub struct ShaderStages: u16 {
   314	        const VERTEX = 0x1;
   315	        const FRAGMENT = 0x2;
   316	        const COMPUTE = 0x4;
   317	        const MESH = 0x8;
   318	        const TASK = 0x10;
   319	        const RAY_GENERATION = 0x20;
   320	        const ANY_HIT = 0x40;
   321	        const CLOSEST_HIT = 0x80;
   322	        const MISS = 0x100;
   323	        const COMPUTE_LIKE = Self::COMPUTE.bits() | Self::TASK.bits() | Self::MESH.bits();
   324	    }
   325	}
   326	
   327	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]
   328	#[cfg_attr(feature = "serialize", derive(serde::Serialize))]
   329	#[cfg_attr(feature = "deserialize", derive(serde::Deserialize))]
   330	pub struct ModuleInfo {
   331	    type_flags: Vec<TypeFlags>,
   332	    functions: Vec<FunctionInfo>,
   333	    entry_points: Vec<FunctionInfo>,
   334	    const_expression_types: Box<[TypeResolution]>,
   335	}
   336	
   337	impl ops::Index<Handle<crate::Type>> for ModuleInfo {
   338	    type Output = TypeFlags;
   339	    fn index(&self, handle: Handle<crate::Type>) -> &Self::Output {
   340	        &self.type_flags[handle.index()]
   341	    }
   342	}
   343	
   344	impl ops::Index<Handle<crate::Function>> for ModuleInfo {
   345	    type Output = FunctionInfo;
   346	    fn index(&self, handle: Handle<crate::Function>) -> &Self::Output {
   347	        &self.functions[handle.index()]
   348	    }
   349	}

  1067	macro_rules! check_extension_validation {
  1068	    ( $caps:expr, $source:expr, $parse_err:expr, $val_err_pat:pat $(, $other_caps:expr)? ) => {
  1069	        #[allow(unused_mut, unused_assignments)]
  1070	        let mut other_caps = naga::valid::Capabilities::empty();
  1071	        $(other_caps = $other_caps;)?
  1072	        let caps = $caps;
  1073	        let source = $source;
  1074	        let mut ext = None;
  1075	        for cap in caps.iter() {
  1076	            match cap.extension() {
  1077	                Some(this_ext) if ext.is_none() => ext = Some(this_ext),
  1078	                Some(this_ext) if ext.is_some_and(|ext| ext != this_ext) => {
  1079	                    panic!(
  1080	                        concat!(
  1081	                            "the capabilities {:?} in `check_extension_validation` ",
  1082	                            "are not all covered by the same extension ",
  1083	                            "(found both {:?} and {:?})",
  1084	                        ),
  1085	                        caps, ext, this_ext,
  1086	                    );
  1087	                }
  1088	                _ => {}
  1089	            }
  1090	        }
  1091	        let Some(ext) = ext else {
  1092	            panic!(
  1093	                concat!(
  1094	                    "None of the capabilities {:?} in `check_extension_validation` ",
  1095	                    "are associated with an extension. ",
  1096	                    "Use `check_validation!` to check validator behavior ",
  1097	                    "when there isn't a corresponding parse error.",
  1098	                ),
  1099	                caps
  1100	            );
  1101	        };
  1102	        let directive = format!(

  1105	        );
  1106	        assert!(

  1108	            "test case for `check_extension_validation!` should not contain the enable directive",
  1109	        );
  1110	
  1111	        // First check, for the expected WGSL parse error when extension is not enabled
  1112	        check(&source, $parse_err);
  1113	        let source_with_enable = format!("{directive}\n{source}");
  1114	        let module = match naga::front::wgsl::parse_str(&source_with_enable) {
  1115	            Ok(module) => module,
  1116	            Err(err) => {
  1117	                eprintln!("WGSL parse failed:");
  1118	                panic!("{}", err.emit_to_string(source));
  1119	            }
  1120	        };
  1121	
  1122	        // Second check, for the expected validation error when the capability is not present
  1123	        // Don't check with explicitly allowed caps, as certain things (currently just

  1144	                stringify!($val_err_pat)
  1145	            );
  1146	            panic!("validation error does not match pattern");
  1147	        }
  1148	
  1149	        // Also check that when multiple capabililiites can enable a feature,

  1154	                    .validate(&module);

Now I understand the pattern. The `check_extension_validation!` macro tests that:
1. Without the `enable` directive, there's a parse error
2. With the `enable` directive but without the capability, there's a validation error

Currently, `binding_array` doesn't have an enable extension, so it doesn't use `check_extension_validation!`. The PR wants to add `enable wgpu_binding_array;` as a requirement.

use naga::front::wgsl::parse_str;

fn main() {
    // Test: binding_array should currently work WITHOUT any enable extension
    let source = r#"
        struct Buffer { data: u32 }
        @group(0) @binding(0)
        var<storage> storage_array: binding_array<Buffer, 10>;
    "#;
    
    match parse_str(source) {
        Ok(module) => {
            println!("PASS: binding_array parsed without enable extension (current behavior)");
            // Now validate
            let mut validator = naga::valid::Validator::new(
                naga::valid::ValidationFlags::all(),
                naga::valid::Capabilities::all(),
            );
            match validator.validate(&module) {
                Ok(_) => println!("  Validation passed"),
                Err(e) => println!("  Validation error: {:?}", e),
            }
        }
        Err(e) => {
            println!("FAIL: binding_array failed to parse: {}", e.emit_to_string(source));
        }
    }
}
EOF

The `capability` method I added returns `C::empty()` for `WgpuBindingArray`. But I need to think about whether we need a new capability. Looking at the existing pattern:
- `enable f16;` requires `SHADER_FLOAT16` capability
- `enable wgpu_mesh_shader;` requires `MESH_SHADER` capability
- `enable wgpu_ray_query;` requires `RAY_QUERY` capability

For `binding_array`, there isn't a single capability that enables all binding arrays. The capabilities are split into:
- `TEXTURE_AND_SAMPLER_BINDING_ARRAY`
- `BUFFER_BINDING_ARRAY`
- `STORAGE_TEXTURE_BINDING_ARRAY`
- `STORAGE_BUFFER_BINDING_ARRAY`
- `ACCELERATION_STRUCTURE_BINDING_ARRAY`

So the `enable wgpu_binding_array;` extension doesn't map to a single capability. It just allows the type to be used in parsing; validation will still check individual capabilities based on what the binding array contains.

  5153	fn check_with_capabilities(input: &str, snapshot: &str, capabilities: Capabilities) {
  5154	    let mut options = naga::front::wgsl::Options::new();
  5155	    options.capabilities = capabilities;
  5156	    let mut frontend = naga::front::wgsl::Frontend::new_with_options(options);
  5157	    let output = match frontend.parse(input) {
  5158	        Ok(_) => panic!("expected parser error, but parsing succeeded!"),
  5159	        Err(err) => err.emit_to_string(input),
  5160	    };
  5161	    if output != snapshot {
  5162	        for diff in diff::lines(snapshot, &output) {
  5163	            match diff {
  5164	                diff::Result::Left(l) => println!("-{l}"),

- `enable f16;` requires `SHADER_FLOAT16` capability
- `enable wgpu_mesh_shader;` requires `MESH_SHADER` capability

But for `binding_array`, there's no single capability. The individual binding array types have separate capabilities (like `TEXTURE_AND_SAMPLER_BINDING_ARRAY`, `BUFFER_BINDING_ARRAY`, etc.).

However, the PR description says to require `enable wgpu_binding_array;` to use `binding_array`. This is purely a parse-time check. The validation capabilities for specific binding array types should remain separate.

But the test `enable_without_capability` expects that EVERY enable extension has a non-empty capability that can be missing. This is a test that needs to be updated.

Since the user said they'll handle test changes, I think my implementation is correct. But let me double-check: maybe we should NOT add `WgpuBindingArray` to `ImplementedEnableExtension::all()` or maybe the test should skip extensions with empty capabilities.

Actually, wait. Let me reconsider. Looking at the PR more carefully, maybe the approach should be different. Perhaps we should not add `WgpuBindingArray` as an `ImplementedEnableExtension` at all, but rather add it as an `UnimplementedEnableExtension`? No, that doesn't make sense.

Let me look at how other similar features work. The `binding_array` is a WGPU-specific feature, just like `wgpu_mesh_shader` and `wgpu_ray_query`. Those require their respective enable extensions. The PR just wants consistency.

I think my implementation is correct. The test failures in non-test files (like the example wgsl files `binding-arrays.wgsl` and `binding-buffer-arrays.wgsl`) need to be updated to include `enable wgpu_binding_array;`. But the user said they'll handle test file changes.

- `TEXTURE_AND_SAMPLER_BINDING_ARRAY` - for binding arrays of textures/samplers
- `BUFFER_BINDING_ARRAY` - for binding arrays of uniform buffers
- `STORAGE_TEXTURE_BINDING_ARRAY` - for binding arrays of storage textures
- `STORAGE_BUFFER_BINDING_ARRAY` - for binding arrays of storage buffers
- `ACCELERATION_STRUCTURE_BINDING_ARRAY` - for binding arrays of acceleration structures

These are checked during validation, not during parsing. The `enable wgpu_binding_array;` is just a parse-time requirement to use the `binding_array` type at all. The validation will still check the individual capabilities based on what's inside the binding array.

So having `WgpuBindingArray` with no capability is correct - it's just a syntactic gate, not a semantic one.

     9	#[derive(Debug, Default)]
    10	pub struct TranslationUnit<'a> {
    11	    pub enable_extensions: EnableExtensions,
    12	    pub decls: Arena<GlobalDecl<'a>>,
    13	    /// The common expressions arena for the entire translation unit.
    14	    ///
    15	    /// All functions, global initializers, array lengths, etc. store their
    16	    /// expressions here. We apportion these out to individual Naga
    17	    /// [`Function`]s' expression arenas at lowering time. Keeping them all in a
    18	    /// single arena simplifies handling of things like array lengths (which are
    19	    /// effectively global and thus don't clearly belong to any function) and
    20	    /// initializers (which can appear in both function-local and module-scope
    21	    /// contexts).
    22	    ///
    23	    /// [`Function`]: crate::Function
    24	    pub expressions: Arena<Expression<'a>>,
    25	
    26	    /// Arena for all diagnostic filter rules parsed in this module, including those in functions.
    27	    ///
    28	    /// See [`DiagnosticFilterNode`] for details on how the tree is represented and used in
    29	    /// validation.
    30	    pub diagnostic_filters: Arena<DiagnosticFilterNode>,
    31	    /// The leaf of all `diagnostic(…)` directives in this module.
    32	    ///
    33	    /// See [`DiagnosticFilterNode`] for details on how the tree is represented and used in
    34	    /// validation.
    35	    pub diagnostic_filter_leaf: Option<Handle<DiagnosticFilterNode>>,
    36	
    37	    /// Doc comments appearing first in the file.
    38	    /// This serves as documentation for the whole TranslationUnit.
    39	    pub doc_comments: Vec<&'a str>,
    40	}
    41	
    42	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy)]
    43	pub struct Ident<'a> {
    44	    pub name: &'a str,
    45	    pub span: Span,
    46	}
    47	
    48	/// An identifier that [resolves] to some declaration.
    49	///
    50	/// This does not cover context-dependent names: attributes, built-in values,
    51	/// and so on. We map those to their Naga IR equivalents as soon as they're
    52	/// parsed, so they never need to appear as identifiers in the AST.
    53	///
    54	/// [resolves]: https://gpuweb.github.io/gpuweb/wgsl/#resolves
    55	#[derive(Debug)]
    56	pub enum IdentExpr<'a> {
    57	    /// An identifier referring to a module-scope declaration or predeclared
    58	    /// object.
    59	    ///
    60	    /// We need to collect the entire module before we can resolve this, to
    61	    /// distinguish between predeclared objects and module-scope declarations
    62	    /// that appear after their uses.
    63	    ///
    64	    /// Whenever you create one of these values, you almost certainly want to
    65	    /// insert the `&str` into [`ExpressionContext::unresolved`][ECu], to ensure
    66	    /// that [indexing] knows that the name's declaration must be lowered before
    67	    /// the one containing this use. Using [`Parser::ident_expr`][ie] to build
    68	    /// `IdentExpr` will take care of that for you.
    69	    ///
    70	    /// [ECu]: super::ExpressionContext::unresolved
    71	    /// [ie]: super::Parser::ident_expr
    72	    /// [indexing]: crate::front::wgsl::index::Index::generate
    73	    Unresolved(&'a str),
    74	
    75	    /// An identifier that has been resolved to a non-module-scope declaration.
    76	    Local(Handle<Local>),
    77	}
    78	
    79	/// An identifier with optional template parameters.
    80	///
    81	/// Following the WGSL specification (see the [`template_list`] non-terminal),
    82	/// `TemplateElaboratedIdent` represents all template parameters as expressions:
    83	/// even parameters to type generators, like the `f32` in `vec3<f32>`, are [Type
    84	/// Expressions].
    85	///
    86	/// # Examples
    87	///
    88	/// - A use of a global variable `colors` would be an [`Expression::Ident(v)`][EI],
    89	///   where `v` is an `TemplateElaboratedIdent` whose `ident` is
    90	///   [`IdentExpr::Unresolved("colors")`][IEU]. Lowering will resolve this to a
    91	///   reference to the global variable.
    92	///
    93	/// - The type `f32` in a variable declaration is represented as a
    94	///   `TemplateElaboratedIdent` whose `ident` is
    95	///   [`IdentExpr::Unresolved("f32")`][IEU]. Lowering will resolve this to
    96	///   WGSL's predeclared `f32` type.
    97	///
    98	/// - The type `vec3<f32>` can be represented as a `TemplateElaboratedIdent`
    99	///   whose `ident` is [`IdentExpr::Unresolved("vec3")`][IEU], and whose
   100	///   `template_list` has one element: an [`ExpressionIdent(v)`][EI] where `v` is a
   101	///   nested `TemplateElaboratedIdent` representing `f32` as described above.
   102	///
   103	/// - The type `array<vec3<f32>, 4>` has `"array"` as its `ident`, and then
   104	///   a two-element `template_list`:
   105	///
   106	///     - `template_list[0]` is an [`Expression::Ident(v)`][EI] where `v` is a nested
   107	///       `TemplateElaboratedIdent` representing `vec3<f32>` as described above.
   108	///
   109	///     - `template_list[1]` is an [`Expression`] representing `4`.
   110	///
   111	/// After [indexing] the module to ensure that declarations appear before uses,
   112	/// lowering can see which declaration a given `TemplateElaboratedIdent`s
   113	/// `ident` refers to. The declaration then determines how to interpret the
   114	/// `template_list`.
   115	///
   116	/// [`template_list`]: https://gpuweb.github.io/gpuweb/wgsl/#syntax-template_list
   117	/// [Type Expressions]: https://gpuweb.github.io/gpuweb/wgsl/#type-expr
   118	/// [IEU]: IdentExpr::Unresolved
   119	/// [EI]: Expression::Ident
   120	/// [indexing]: crate::front::wgsl::index::Index::generate
   121	#[derive(Debug)]
   122	pub struct TemplateElaboratedIdent<'a> {
   123	    pub ident: IdentExpr<'a>,
   124	    pub ident_span: Span,
   125	
   126	    /// If non-empty, the template parameters following the identifier.
   127	    pub template_list: Vec<Handle<Expression<'a>>>,
   128	    pub template_list_span: Span,
   129	}
   130	
   131	/// A function call or value constructor expression.
   132	///
   133	/// We can't tell whether an expression like `IDENTIFIER(EXPR, ...)` is a
   134	/// construction expression or a function call until we know `IDENTIFIER`'s
   135	/// definition, so we represent everything of that form as one of these
   136	/// expressions until lowering. At that point, [`Lowerer::call`] has
   137	/// everything's definition in hand, and can decide whether to emit a Naga
   138	/// [`Constant`], [`As`], [`Splat`], or [`Compose`] expression.
   139	///
   140	/// [`Lowerer::call`]: Lowerer::call
   141	/// [`Constant`]: crate::Expression::Constant
   142	/// [`As`]: crate::Expression::As
   143	/// [`Splat`]: crate::Expression::Splat
   144	/// [`Compose`]: crate::Expression::Compose
   145	#[derive(Debug)]
   146	pub struct CallPhrase<'a> {
   147	    pub function: TemplateElaboratedIdent<'a>,
   148	    pub arguments: Vec<Handle<Expression<'a>>>,
   149	}
   150	
   151	/// A reference to a module-scope definition or predeclared object.
   152	///
   153	/// Each [`GlobalDecl`] holds a set of these values, to be resolved to
   154	/// specific definitions later. To support de-duplication, `Eq` and
   155	/// `Hash` on a `Dependency` value consider only the name, not the
   156	/// source location at which the reference occurs.
   157	#[derive(Debug)]
   158	pub struct Dependency<'a> {
   159	    /// The name referred to.
   160	    pub ident: &'a str,
   161	
   162	    /// The location at which the reference to that name occurs.
   163	    pub usage: Span,
   164	}
   165	
   166	impl Hash for Dependency<'_> {
   167	    fn hash<H: core::hash::Hasher>(&self, state: &mut H) {
   168	        self.ident.hash(state);
   169	    }
   170	}
   171	
   172	impl PartialEq for Dependency<'_> {
   173	    fn eq(&self, other: &Self) -> bool {
   174	        self.ident == other.ident
   175	    }
   176	}
   177	
   178	impl Eq for Dependency<'_> {}
   179	
   180	/// A module-scope declaration.
   181	#[derive(Debug)]
   182	pub struct GlobalDecl<'a> {
   183	    pub kind: GlobalDeclKind<'a>,
   184	
   185	    /// Names of all module-scope or predeclared objects this
   186	    /// declaration uses.
   187	    pub dependencies: FastIndexSet<Dependency<'a>>,
   188	}
   189	
   190	#[derive(Debug)]
   191	pub enum GlobalDeclKind<'a> {
   192	    Fn(Function<'a>),
   193	    Var(GlobalVariable<'a>),
   194	    Const(Const<'a>),
   195	    Override(Override<'a>),
   196	    Struct(Struct<'a>),
   197	    Type(TypeAlias<'a>),
   198	    ConstAssert(Handle<Expression<'a>>),
   199	}
   200	
   201	#[derive(Debug)]
   202	pub struct FunctionArgument<'a> {
   203	    pub name: Ident<'a>,
   204	    pub ty: TemplateElaboratedIdent<'a>,
   205	    pub binding: Option<Binding<'a>>,
   206	    pub handle: Handle<Local>,
   207	}
   208

   210	pub struct FunctionResult<'a> {
   211	    pub ty: TemplateElaboratedIdent<'a>,
   212	    pub binding: Option<Binding<'a>>,
   213	    pub must_use: bool,
   214	}
   215	
   216	#[derive(Debug)]

   220	    pub workgroup_size: Option<[Option<Handle<Expression<'a>>>; 3]>,
   221	    pub mesh_output_variable: Option<(&'a str, Span)>,
   222	    pub task_payload: Option<(&'a str, Span)>,
   223	    pub ray_incoming_payload: Option<(&'a str, Span)>,
   224	}
   225

   237	    pub doc_comments: Vec<&'a str>,
   238	}

   172	        features.contains(wgt::Features::MEMORY_DECORATION_COHERENT),
   173	    );
   174	    caps.set(
   175	        Caps::MEMORY_DECORATION_VOLATILE,
   176	        features.contains(wgt::Features::MEMORY_DECORATION_VOLATILE),
   177	    );
   178	    caps
   179	}
   180	
   181	/// Create a [`naga::valid::Validator`] configured for the given feature set.
   182	pub fn create_validator(
   183	    features: wgt::Features,
   184	    downlevel: wgt::DownlevelFlags,
   185	    flags: naga::valid::ValidationFlags,
   186	) -> naga::valid::Validator {
   187	    let caps = features_to_naga_capabilities(features, downlevel);
   188	    naga::valid::Validator::new(flags, caps)
   189	}
   190	
   191	/// Map a [`wgt::TextureFormat`] to the corresponding [`naga::StorageFormat`], if any.
   192	pub fn map_storage_format_to_naga(format: wgt::TextureFormat) -> Option<naga::StorageFormat> {
   193	    use naga::StorageFormat as Sf;
   194	    use wgt::TextureFormat as Tf;
   195

   197	        Tf::R8Unorm => Sf::R8Unorm,

   199	        Tf::R8Uint => Sf::R8Uint,

   208	        Tf::Rg8Sint => Sf::Rg8Sint,

   213	        Tf::Rg16Uint => Sf::Rg16Uint,
   214	        Tf::Rg16Sint => Sf::Rg16Sint,

   216	        Tf::Rgba8Unorm => Sf::Rgba8Unorm,
   217	        Tf::Rgba8Snorm => Sf::Rgba8Snorm,
   218	        Tf::Rgba8Uint => Sf::Rgba8Uint,

   246	    })
   247	}

   305	/// Map a [`naga::ShaderStage`] to the corresponding [`wgt::ShaderStages`] flag.
   306	pub fn map_naga_stage(stage: naga::ShaderStage) -> wgt::ShaderStages {
   307	    match stage {
   308	        naga::ShaderStage::Vertex => wgt::ShaderStages::VERTEX,
   309	        naga::ShaderStage::Fragment => wgt::ShaderStages::FRAGMENT,
   310	        naga::ShaderStage::Compute => wgt::ShaderStages::COMPUTE,
   311	        naga::ShaderStage::Task => wgt::ShaderStages::TASK,
   312	        naga::ShaderStage::Mesh => wgt::ShaderStages::MESH,
   313	        naga::ShaderStage::RayGeneration => wgt::ShaderStages::RAY_GENERATION,
   314	        naga::ShaderStage::AnyHit => wgt::ShaderStages::ANY_HIT,
   315	        naga::ShaderStage::ClosestHit => wgt::ShaderStages::CLOSEST_HIT,
   316	        naga::ShaderStage::Miss => wgt::ShaderStages::MISS,
   317	    }
   318	}

use naga::front::wgsl::parse_str;

fn main() {
    // Test 1: binding_array WITHOUT enable should fail
    let source = r#"
        struct Buffer { data: u32 }
        @group(0) @binding(0)
        var<storage> storage_array: binding_array<Buffer, 10>;
    "#;
    
    match parse_str(source) {
        Ok(_) => println!("FAIL: binding_array parsed without enable directive"),
        Err(e) => println!("PASS: binding_array rejected without enable: {}", e.emit_to_string(source).lines().next().unwrap()),
    }
    
    // Test 2: binding_array WITH enable should succeed
    let source2 = r#"
        enable wgpu_binding_array;
        struct Buffer { data: u32 }
        @group(0) @binding(0)
        var<storage> storage_array: binding_array<Buffer, 10>;
    "#;
    
    match parse_str(source2) {
        Ok(module) => {
            println!("PASS: binding_array parsed with enable directive");
            // Now validate
            let mut validator = naga::valid::Validator::new(
                naga::valid::ValidationFlags::all(),
                naga::valid::Capabilities::all(),
            );
            match validator.validate(&module) {
                Ok(_) => println!("  Validation passed"),
                Err(e) => println!("  Validation error: {:?}", e),
            }
        }
        Err(e) => {
            println!("FAIL: binding_array with enable failed: {}", e.emit_to_string(source2));
        }
    }
    
    // Test 3: unknown extension should still fail
    let source3 = r#"
        enable wgpu_nonexistent;
    "#;
    
    match parse_str(source3) {
        Ok(_) => println!("FAIL: unknown extension accepted"),
        Err(e) => println!("PASS: unknown extension rejected: {}", e.emit_to_string(source3).lines().next().unwrap()),
    }
}
EOF
